<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">teddybear</i>. Named after <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Theodore_Roosevelt" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Theodore Roosevelt">Theodore Roosevelt</a>, who <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> nicknamed "<a href = vnd.unilang:teddy.html>Teddy</a>".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***teder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a> (11924)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">teeder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tidar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tidaraz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de"><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fine; delicate; thin; sensitive; tender; weak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tear</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weak; not strong</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tidder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>tederder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">tederst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>delicate, dainty</li>
<li>sensitive, tender, easily hurt or damaged</li>
<li>gentle, tender, with care
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tilde.html>tilde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hield.html>hield</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> palm <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> hand.</i>
<dl><dd>He raised her up and <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> her <b>tenderly</b> in the palm of his hand.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a></b>  <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">teve</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tiva</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tibō-</i>.
</p><p>Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tife</i> and probably <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zibbe</i>.

***teek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teek.html>teek</a> (25574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:West Germanic languages">West Germanic</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tīkkô</i>, suffixed variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tīgô</i>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tick</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zecke</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teek.html>teek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teken.html>teken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teek.html>teekje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tick <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">insect</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***teer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a> (10479)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>tar</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">têer</i>, alternative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">têder</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">têeder</i> (whence modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tidar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tidaraz</i>; cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">teere</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>tenderness</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teerder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">teerst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tender, delicate</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teren.html>teren</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teren.html>teren</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>Over</a> time, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> also used to refer to tuberculosis, analogously to English consumption.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>the act of digesting or being consumed</li>
<li>tuberculosis</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology 5</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tree</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*trio</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*treo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*trewą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tree, wood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Pre-Germanic *<i>dréu̯om</i>, thematic e-grade derivative of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dóru</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tree</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tree</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">træ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teren.html>teren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tree</li></ol>

***teerling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teerling.html>teerling</a> (48359)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">terne</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">double three</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> but <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> dissimilated with the <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ling</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teerling.html>teerling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teerlingen.html>teerlingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teerling.html>teerlinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">dice</span>, polyhedron used in games of chance</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In modern language, only used as a part of fixed phrase '<b><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:teerling.html>teerling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geworpen.html>geworpen</a>'</b> (<i>the <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> cast</i>).

***tegel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegel.html>tegel</a> (32985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tigele</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegel.html>tegel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tegela</i>, from late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tigulǭ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tegula</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ziegel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tile</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegel.html>tegel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegels.html>tegels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegeltje.html>tegeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tile</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tichel.html>tichel</a></span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tehuis.html>tehuis</a> (7458)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> huus</i>; equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tehuis.html>tehuis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tehuizen.html>tehuizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tehuis.html>tehuisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>home, asylum</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Whereas <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a></i> refers to one's home as a place of residence, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:tehuis.html>tehuis</a></i> refers to an asylum or refuge where one may or may not feel at home.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tehuis.html>tehuis</a></strong>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teken.html>teken</a> (989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">têken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tēkan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taikną</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">têkenen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tēkanen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taiknijaną</i>.
